| <span data-ttu-id="87be9-457">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87be9-457">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="87be9-458">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87be9-458">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="87be9-1703">Comentários</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87be9-1703">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="87be9-1704">A classe **MS-DFSR-** teleclass é parte do suporte do serviço de replicação do sistema de arquivos distribuído (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="87be9-1704">The **ms-DFSR-ReplicationGroup** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
